The room was not a big one but very cosy and comfortable. It was clean and well equipped with all sort of accessories that we need. Overall our two nights stay were really pleasant and comfortable. We would definitely book this hotel again when we visit Guangzhou next time. One special thank you is to be given to Cion Hu who helped us to settle down quickly upon check in.

Due to the small number of people, the executive lounge is not open, so the executive reception is in the lobby. HH is a set meal. The staple food on the first night is fried dumplings and fried spring rolls. I had no desire to eat it the next day.
The room has no view at all, surrounded by tall buildings, basically facing the river view.
It can only be said that there is no harm if there is no comparison, because I came from the Aoyuan Sheraton the night before, and the room and the other party did not have a lounge. The service is really bad, but the price is not much different.
Probably the last time to visit this hotel. For this price, I personally recommend going to the Westin next door, at least the room is much more comfortable.

msg:The hotel is adjacent to the Canton Fair Complex. It is about a 10-minute walk from Xingang East Station to the hotel. It is very convenient for green travel or self-driving. It takes about 15 minutes to drive to Huangpu Ancient Port, Padi, Canton Tower, etc. The geographical location is related to the lack of life in the surrounding area. There are fewer restaurants, convenience stores, etc.
The hotel combines modern elegance and urban charm, with a strong sense of design, novel and unique, and it is worth visiting everywhere. Although it is a hotel opened in 13 years, the overall maintenance is good. The lobby is located on the fourth floor. The front desk has a friendly service attitude. The check-in speed is fast. Disposable toiletries can be collected at the front desk. Members can check out for free. You can also ask if you can upgrade the room.
What is more satisfactory is that all functional areas are concentrated on the fourth floor, eliminating the trouble of switching between layers. The gym and indoor swimming pool are hidden in the Chuan Spa. The gym is not big, with complete equipment and newer equipment. The indoor constant temperature swimming pool has good water quality, and there are slightly more people during the summer. The Langham Club is on the 22nd floor. Guests staying in executive rooms can check in and check out here. The service is good and comfortable. They can enjoy happy hour and other exclusive services here. Chatting and blowing hair is very comfortable.
I stayed in an executive room on that day. The corridor with the back-shaped structure has quite a visual impact. The room is large, the environment is comfortable, low-key and elegant, and the large floor-to-ceiling windows provide a wide field of vision. However, the scenery of Huangpu Chung is not very good. The curtains are electric, only It can be fully turned on and off, the room facilities are all available, there are many types of pillows, the mattress is mousse, I have to say that it is very comfortable, I can sleep in seconds for those who recognize the bed, and the room has good sound insulation, and the air conditioner operates very quietly. Corridor carpets also effectively reduce noise, which is a blessing for light sleepers! But there is no socket by the bed. The washroom and shower room are large and the water pressure is sufficient, but the bathtub is slightly smaller. The shower gel, shampoo, etc. are its own brand "Chuan" SPA. The rosemary series is quite soothing, and it feels okay to use. The only downside is the washroom. There is no clothes basket, and the hooks are not enough. I don't know where to put the towels and bath towels after use. In addition, the bathroom is only separated from the outside world by glass, which is a little embarrassing.
The overall check-in experience is good, the service is in place, the guest is at home, and the price-performance ratio is high. If non-business people have a demand for the exhibition, it is quite suitable for weekend relaxation.

The overall feeling is good, quiet and safe.
Location: Near the Canton Plaza, the subway Xingang East Station, but not directly on the subway, it takes 5-6 minutes to get out of the subway. It is recommended to come by car, guests can park for free.

Environment: The overall business minimalist style, the lobby is not luxurious. The lobby is on the fourth floor, and there is an internet celebrity afternoon tea set, but there are not many tables and chairs, so you should book it in advance. There are three types of tables and chairs in the lobby, but I feel that the tables and chairs are too crowded. But for business, privacy is normal.

Facilities: There is a heated swimming pool, SPA. Didn't experience this part this time.

Safety: You need to swipe the room card to enter the guest room, which is safe and secure.

Guest room: This time, the [River View King Room] has been upgraded. Although the scenery is not Linjiang, it is separated from the Canton Fair in front, and you still feel the business aura. The room has a bathtub, but the size is a single person.

Service: The front desk is very polite, and can generally meet any special small requirements, such as checking out the room status and delaying check-out for a few hours. In the guest room, I also called several times to ask for mineral water, edible ice cubes, and free shoe shine service. [Naughty]

Catering: There is afternoon tea in the lobby in the afternoon, and there is a buffet restaurant (but the category is average). The buffet breakfast is added at the time of temporary check-in, which is more expensive. If you make a reservation, you can add it in advance on some platforms in advance. The tables and chairs are also a little crowded. I feel that during the non-business season, there are not many people in the restaurant anyway, so there is no need to put them so crowded. . . . I don't understand, maybe there are a lot of people during the business exhibition?
Western restaurants and Michelin-recommended restaurants may be tried, but buffets are fine (maybe I have higher requirements for buffets)

The skybar is a good place to take pictures, but it's too cold at night. Maybe summer is a great place to drink. There were 300 minus 100 vouchers at the Spring Festival, I don't know if there will be any more in the future


Overall, suitable for business people. Usually the price is not high, if you go on a leisure vacation, you can find a place for cost-effectiveness. But not resort style.
